# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

Perfect! I have successfully completed the analysis of gRPC error status propagation across the three repositories. Here's a summary of what I found:

## Summary

I've created `/workspace/answer.json` with comprehensive findings on how gRPC error status codes are created and propagated to HTTP responses across **kubernetes/kubernetes**, **etcd-io/etcd**, and **grafana/grafana**.

### Key Findings:

**Kubernetes:**
- Creates gRPC errors at service boundaries with codes like `codes.NotFound`, `codes.Internal`, `codes.ResourceExhausted`
- Translates to HTTP via `WriteError()` and grpc-gateway's `HTTPStatusFromCode()` 
- Uses distributed error creation pattern

**etcd:**
- Centralizes all gRPC error definitions in `api/v3rpc/rpctypes/error.go`
- Uses explicit `toGRPCErrorMap` for domain-to-gRPC error translation in `server/etcdserver/api/v3rpc/util.go`
- Implements gRPC interceptors for server-side error handling

**Grafana:**
- Creates gRPC errors at service boundaries
- Uses grpc-gateway middleware with custom error handlers for HTTP translation
- Implements error source detection for downstream vs local errors

### Output Structure:
The answer.json contains:
- **26 files** from all three repos with relevant gRPC error handling code
- **21 symbols** (functions/types) that create or translate gRPC errors
- **6 key functions** showing the error propagation chain
- **Detailed narrative** explaining each repo's approach and key differences

Pattern:**\\nKubernetes creates gRPC errors at service boundaries. Core translation function:\\n  - `codes.NotFound` \u2192 `http.StatusNotFound`\\n  - `codes.ResourceExhausted` \u2192 `http.StatusTooManyRequests`\\n  - Default \u2192 `http.StatusInternalServerError`\\n\\n- `vendor/github.com/grpc-ecosystem/grpc-gateway/v2/runtime/errors.go:HTTPStatusFromCode()` - Business logic in etcdserver generates domain errors\\n2. `server/etcdserver/api/v3rpc/util.go:togRPCError()` converts to gRPC status errors\\n3. `server/etcdserver/api/v3rpc/interceptor.go` - unary and stream interceptors enforce capabilities and return errors\\n4. `client/v3/retry_interceptor.go:contextErrToGRPCErr()` - client-side handler converts context errors to gRPC status\\n5. HTTP handlers in `peer.go` translate to HTTP status codes\\n\\n### Grafana (grafana/grafana)\\n\\n**Error Creation Pattern:**\\nGrafana creates gRPC errors at service boundaries:\\n- `pkg/services/authz/rbac/service.go:ListPermission()` - `status.Error(codes.NotFound, \\\"unsupported resource\\\")`\\n- Service implementation returns gRPC status errors directly\\n\\n**HTTP Translation Pattern:**\\nGrafana uses grpc-gateway middleware to convert gRPC errors:\\n- `pkg/services/authz/zanzana/server/openfga_server.go:NewOpenFGAHttpServer()` uses:\\n  - `runtime.WithErrorHandler()` - Custom HTTP error handler\\n  - `runtime.WithStreamErrorHandler()` - Stream error handler\\n  - Calls `serverErrors.ConvertToEncodedErrorCode(status.Convert(e))` to convert gRPC status\\n  - Calls `httpmiddleware.CustomHTTPErrorHandler()` to write HTTP response\\n\\n- `pkg/storage/unified/resource/errors.go:HTTPStatusFromCode()` - Maps gRPC codes to HTTP:\\n  - Uses `runtime.HTTPStatusFromCode(st.Code())` for standard mapping\\n  - Falls back to `500` for unmapped codes\\n\\n**Error Propagation Chain:**\\n1. Service methods return gRPC status errors\\n2. `pkg/tsdb/influxdb/fsql/fsql.go:Query()` - Receives gRPC errors from FlightSQL client\\n3. `ErrGRPCCorrupt = status.Error(codes.DataLoss, ...)`\\n\\n**HTTP Translation Pattern:**\\netcd uses `toGRPCErrorMap` to translate internal errors to gRPC errors in `server/etcdserver/api/v3rpc/util.go:togRPCError()`:\\n- Maps domain errors (e.g., `membership.ErrIDNotFound`) to gRPC status errors\\n- Falls back to `status.Error(codes.Unknown, ...)` for unmapped errors\\n- Handles context errors specially: `context.Canceled` and `context.DeadlineExceeded` are passed through\\n\\nHTTP responses are handled in `server/etcdserver/api/etcdhttp/peer.go`:\\n- `membership.ErrIDNotFound` \u2192 `http.StatusNotFound`\\n- `membership.ErrMemberNotLearner` \u2192 `http.StatusPreconditionFailed`\\n- `errors.ErrLearnerNotReady` \u2192 `http.StatusPreconditionFailed`\\n\\n**Error Propagation Chain:**\\n1. Business logic in etcdserver generates domain errors\\n2. `server/etcdserver/api/v3rpc/util.go:togRPCError()` converts to gRPC status errors\\n3. `server/etcdserver/api/v3rpc/interceptor.go` - unary and stream interceptors enforce capabilities and return errors\\n4. `client/v3/retry_interceptor.go:contextErrToGRPCErr()` - client-side handler converts context errors to gRPC status\\n5. HTTP handlers in `peer.go` translate to HTTP status codes\\n\\n### Grafana (grafana/grafana)\\n\\n**Error Creation Pattern:**\\nGrafana creates gRPC errors at service boundaries:\\n- `pkg/services/authz/rbac/service.go:ListPermission()` - `status.Error(codes.NotFound, \\\"unsupported resource\\\")`\\n- Service implementation returns gRPC status errors directly\\n\\n**HTTP Translation Pattern:**\\nGrafana uses grpc-gateway middleware to convert gRPC errors:\\n- `pkg/services/authz/zanzana/server/openfga_server.go:NewOpenFGAHttpServer()` uses:\\n  - `runtime.WithErrorHandler()` - Custom HTTP error handler\\n  - `runtime.WithStreamErrorHandler()` - Stream error handler\\n  - Calls `serverErrors.ConvertToEncodedErrorCode(status.Convert(e))` to convert gRPC status\\n  - Calls `httpmiddleware.CustomHTTPErrorHandler()` to write HTTP response\\n\\n- `pkg/storage/unified/resource/errors.go:HTTPStatusFromCode()` - Maps gRPC codes to HTTP:\\n  - Uses `runtime.HTTPStatusFromCode(st.Code())` for standard mapping\\n  - Falls back to `500` for unmapped codes\\n\\n**Error Propagation Chain:**\\n1. Service methods return gRPC status errors\\n2. `pkg/tsdb/influxdb/fsql/fsql.go:Query()` - Receives gRPC errors from FlightSQL client\\n3. Checks `status.FromError(err)` and switches on `grpcStatusErr.Code()`:\\n   - `codes.InvalidArgument` \u2192 `backend.StatusBadRequest`\\n   - `codes.PermissionDenied` \u2192 `backend.StatusForbidden`\\n   - `codes.NotFound` \u2192 `backend.StatusNotFound`\\n   - `codes.Unavailable` \u2192 `http.StatusServiceUnavailable`\\n   - `codes.Unauthenticated` \u2192 `backend.StatusUnauthorized`\\n   - Default \u2192 `backend.StatusInternal`\\n4. grpc-gateway middleware translates to HTTP before returning to client\\n5. `pkg/plugins/manager/client/client.go` - Handles `codes.Canceled` for request cancellation\\n6. `pkg/plugins/backendplugin/grpcplugin/client_v2.go:handleGrpcStatusError()` - Error source handling\\n\\n### Key Patterns and Differences\\n\\n**Centralized vs Distributed Error Creation:**\\n- **etcd**: Centralized in `rpctypes/error.go` - all gRPC errors defined once\\n- **Kubernetes**: Distributed at call sites - errors created where needed\\n- **Grafana**: Mix - some pre-defined, some created at call sites\\n\\n**Error Mapping Strategies:**\\n- **etcd**: Explicit `toGRPCErrorMap` for domain-to-gRPC conversion\\n- **Kubernetes**: Use grpc-gateway's built-in HTTP status mapping\\n- **Grafana**: Custom middleware with `status.Convert()` and error handler callbacks\\n\\n**Propagation Mechanisms:**\\n- **etcd**: Context errors flow through interceptors unchanged; handled separately\\n- **Kubernetes**: Direct mapping at HTTP boundaries via `WriteError()`\\n- **Grafana**: grpc-gateway middleware abstracts the translation\\n\\n**Code Organization:**\\n- **etcd**: Clear separation in `rpctypes/error.go` (creation) and `v3rpc/util.go` (translation)\\n- **Kubernetes**: Vendored grpc-gateway handles translation; service code creates errors\\n- **Grafana**: Service code creates errors; gateway middleware handles translation\"\n}\n",
